CREATE TABLE PMIS_ADM.UIItems(UIItemID number NOT NULL,
                              UIKey varchar2(500),
                              UIName varchar2(300),
                              ParentUIItemID number,
                              CanSetAccessOnlyOwnData number
                             );

ALTER TABLE PMIS_ADM.UIItems ADD CONSTRAINT UIITEMS_PK PRIMARY KEY(UIItemID);
ALTER TABLE PMIS_ADM.UIItems ADD CONSTRAINT UIITEMS_UIITEMS_FK FOREIGN KEY (ParentUIItemID) REFERENCES PMIS_ADM.UIItems (UIItemID);
ALTER TABLE PMIS_ADM.UIItems ADD CONSTRAINT UIITEMS_UNQ UNIQUE (UIKey);

CREATE SEQUENCE PMIS_ADM.UIITEMS_ID_SEQ
START WITH 1 
INCREMENT BY 1 
NOMAXVALUE;

CREATE TRIGGER PMIS_ADM.TRG_UIITEMS_INSERT
BEFORE INSERT ON PMIS_ADM.UIItems
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN
   SELECT PMIS_ADM.UIITEMS_ID_SEQ.nextval INTO :new.UIItemID FROM dual;
END;
/
